<DESCRIPTION>EXHIBIT 99.1
<TEXT>
<html>
  <head>
    <title>acl6k0309acrysoftoric991.htm</title>

    <body bgcolor="#ffffff" style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><br><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Exhibit
99.1</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="left"><img src="acl6k0309acrysoftoric9910.jpg" alt=""></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">New
AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#174;</font>
IQ Toric IOL Approved for U.S. Patients with Cataracts and
Astigmatism</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Innovative
lens provides better distance vision for cataract surgery patients.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland</font> <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#8211; March 2, 2009 &#8211; </font>Alcon, Inc.
(NYSE: ACL), the world&#8217;s leader in eye care and cataract surgery announced that
the U.S. Food and Drug Administration (FDA) approved its aspheric AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> IQ<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>Toric intraocular lens
(IOL).&#160;&#160;The new lens offers an enhanced aspheric optic that improves
image quality and increases contrast sensitivity in cataract surgery patients
with astigmatism. The innovative lens design<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"> offers these patients the
best opportunity for quality distance vision without
glasses.</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#8220;With
the addition of asphericity to the AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Toric
lens, which was already my lens of choice for astigmatic patients, I can now
reduce spherical aberration, enhance image quality and improve functional vision
for my cataract patients,&#8221; said Edward Holland, M.D., director of cornea at the
Cincinnati Eye Institute<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</font>and professor of
ophthalmology at the University of Cincinnati. &#8220;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">At the same time, the
thinner lens profile is ideally suited for micro-coaxial surgical
techniques</font>, which surgeons use to reduce incision size in cataract
surgery.&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>The first AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Toric
lens was introduced in 2005 and quickly became the leading toric lens on the
market, due to its predictable power outcomes and excellent rotational
stability. These benefits are largely realized due to the strengths of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AcrySof</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"> IOL material and
proprietary single-piece design</font>.&#160;&#160;As the first acrylic
single-piece lens, AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> provides
unequalled stability in the eye.&#160;&#160;This is especially important when
correcting astigmatism, which occurs due to an irregular shape of the eye.
Continual innovation of the AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> IOL
platform has characterized the brand, with nearly two decades of product
introductions that have steadily advanced the standard of cataract treatment,
including blue-light filtration, aspheric optics, presbyopia correction and
astigmatic correction.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>&#8220;The AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> IQ<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>Toric IOL is yet another
intraocular lens technology innovation, that is part of Alcon&#8217;s product
development strategy to provide cataract surgeons with tools for customized
treatment based on individual patient needs,&#8221; said Bill Barton, Alcon&#8217;s
president of U.S. operations. &#8220;To that end, Alcon continues to combine multiple
technologies and optics into each new lens introduction, all based on
AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font>, the
world&#8217;s most frequently implanted IOL material.&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>Alcon will commercially launch the new
AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> IQ<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>Toric IOL at the 2009
American Society of Cataract and Refractive Surgeons (ASCRS) annual meeting in
San Francisco, California.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#174;</font>
Intraocular Lenses</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon&#8217;s
AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font>
intraocular lenses are the most frequently implanted lenses in the world, with
more than 40 million implants since their introduction in the early
1990s.&#160;&#160;Alcon&#8217;s AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> IOL
platform offers cataract patients a variety of benefits and is available with a
variety of optics designed to help patients achieve the best possible
vision.&#160;&#160;The AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> family
of IOLs includes the AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> IQ,
AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> IQ Toric
and AcrySof<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> IQ
ReSTOR<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font>
IOLs.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-more-</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">&#160;</div>

        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">&#160;</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Cataract Surgery and Astigmatism</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">A
cataract is a &#8220;clouding&#8221; of the eye&#8217;s natural lens, which results in blurred or
defocused vision.&#160;&#160;IOLs are implanted during cataract surgery to
replace the patient&#8217;s natural lens that has been removed during surgery.
Cataracts cannot be prevented and are the leading cause of treatable blindness
worldwide.&#160;&#160;Corneal astigmatism is an irregularity of the cornea that
can cause significantly blurred or distorted vision.&#160;&#160;For more
information, visit <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.cataractsurgery.com</font>.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Alcon</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon,
Inc. is the world&#8217;s leading eye care company, with sales of approximately $6.3
billion in 2008.&#160;&#160;Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic
industry for 60 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets
pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contact lens care solutions and
other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions
of the eye. Alcon&#8217;s majority shareholder is Nestl&#233;, S.A., the world&#8217;s largest
food company.&#160;&#160;For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the
Company&#8217;s web site at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.alcon.com</font>.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"># #
